    <div style="text-align: justify;">Item 1.<font style="display: inline-block; text-indent: 0px; font-size: 1px; width: 108pt" id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab">&#160;</font><u>Security and Issuer</u></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">This Amendment No. 21 to Schedule 13D on the Common Stock of Cincinnati Bell Inc. (the &#8220;Issuer&#8221;) is being filed on behalf of the undersigned to amend the Schedule 13D, as amended (the &#8220;Schedule 13D&#8221;)
      which was originally filed on January 9, 2008.&#160; Unless otherwise indicated, all capitalized terms used herein but not defined herein shall have the same meanings as set forth in the Schedule 13D.</div>
    <div><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left;">Item 2.<font style="display: inline-block; text-indent: 0px; font-size: 1px; width: 108pt" id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab">&#160;</font><u>Identity and Background</u></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; margin-left: 36pt;">Item 2 to Schedule 13D is amended, in pertinent part, as follows:</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; margin-left: 36pt;">This statement is being filed by Mario J. Gabelli (&#8220;Mario Gabelli&#8221;) and various entities which he</div>
    <div style="text-align: left;">directly or indirectly controls or for which he acts as chief investment officer.&#160; These entities, except for LICT Corporation (&#8220;LICT) and CIBL, Inc. (&#8220;CIBL&#8221;), engage in various aspects of the securities business,
      primarily as investment adviser to various institutional and individual clients, including registered investment companies and pension plans, and as general partner or the equivalent of various private investment partnerships or private funds and as
      a registered broker-dealer.&#160; Certain of these entities may also make investments for their own accounts.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">The foregoing persons in the aggregate often own beneficially more than 5% of a class of equity securities of a particular issuer.&#160; Although several of the foregoing persons are treated as institutional
      investors for purposes of reporting their beneficial ownership on the short-form Schedule 13G, the holdings of those who do not qualify as institutional investors may exceed the 1% threshold presented for filing on Schedule 13G or implementation of
      their investment philosophy may from time to time require action which could be viewed as not completely passive.&#160; In order to avoid any question as to whether their beneficial ownership is being reported on the proper form and in order to provide
      greater investment flexibility and administrative uniformity, these persons have decided to file their beneficial ownership reports on the more detailed Schedule 13D form rather than on the short-form Schedule 13G and thereby to provide more
      expansive disclosure than may be necessary.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">(a), (b) and (c) - This statement is being filed by one or more of the following persons: GGCP, Inc.&#160; (&#8220;GGCP&#8221;), GGCP Holdings LLC (&#8220;GGCP Holdings&#8221;), GAMCO Investors, Inc. (&#8220;GBL&#8221;), Associated Capital
      Group, Inc. (&#8220;AC&#8221;), Gabelli Funds, LLC (&#8220;Gabelli Funds&#8221;), GAMCO Asset Management Inc. (&#8220;GAMCO&#8221;), Teton Advisors, Inc. (&#8220;Teton Advisors&#8221;), Gabelli &amp; Company Investment Advisers, Inc. (&#8220;GCIA&#8221;), Morgan Group Holding Co., (&#8220;MGH&#8221;), G.research, LLC
      (&#8220;G.research&#8221;), MJG Associates, Inc. (&#8220;MJG Associates&#8221;), Gabelli Foundation, Inc. (&#8220;Foundation&#8221;), Mario Gabelli, LICT and CIBL.&#160; Those of the foregoing persons signing this Schedule 13D are hereinafter referred to as the &#8220;Reporting Persons&#8221;.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">GGCP makes investments for its own account and is the manager and a member of GGCP Holdings which is the controlling shareholder of GBL and AC.&#160; GBL, a public company listed on the New York Stock
      Exchange, is the parent company for a variety of companies engaged in the securities business, including certain of those named below.&#160; AC, a public company listed on the New York Stock Exchange, is the parent company for a variety of companies
      engaged in the securities business, including certain of those listed below.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">GAMCO, a wholly-owned subsidiary of GBL, is an investment adviser registered under the Investment Advisers Act of 1940, as amended (&#8220;Advisers Act&#8221;).&#160; GAMCO is an investment manager providing
      discretionary managed account services for employee benefit plans, private investors, endowments, foundations and others.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">GCIA, a wholly owned subsidiary of AC, is an investment adviser registered under the Advisers Act and serves as a general partner or investment manager to limited partnerships and offshore investment
      companies and other accounts.&#160; As a part of its business, GCIA may purchase or sell securities for its own account.&#160; GCIA is a general partner or investment manager of a number of funds or partnerships, including Gabelli Associates Fund, L.P.,
      Gabelli Associates Fund II, L.P., Gabelli Associates Limited, Gabelli Associates Limited II E, ALCE Partners, L.P., Gabelli Capital Structure Arbitrage Fund LP, Gabelli Capital Structure Arbitrage Fund Limited, Gabelli Intermediate Credit Fund L.P.,
      GAMA Select Energy + L.P., GAMCO Medical Opportunities L.P., and Gabelli Multimedia Partners, L.P.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">G.research is a wholly owned subsidiary of MGH.&#160; MGH in turn is controlled by AC through an 83% ownership interest.&#160; G.research, is a broker-dealer registered under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934,
      as amended (&#8220;1934 Act&#8221;), which as a part of its business regularly purchases and sells securities for its own account.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">Gabelli Funds, a wholly owned subsidiary of GBL, is a limited liability company. Gabelli Funds is an investment adviser registered under the Advisers Act which provides advisory services for The Gabelli
      Equity Trust Inc., The Gabelli Asset Fund, The GAMCO Growth Fund, The Gabelli Convertible and Income Securities Fund Inc., The Gabelli Value 25 Fund Inc., The Gabelli Small Cap Growth Fund, The Gabelli Equity Income Fund, The Gabelli ABC Fund, The
      GAMCO Global Content &amp; Connectivity Fund, The Gabelli Gold Fund, Inc., The Gabelli Multimedia Trust Inc., The Gabelli Global Rising Income &amp; Dividend Fund, The Gabelli Capital Asset Fund, The GAMCO International Growth Fund, Inc., The GAMCO
      Global Growth Fund, The Gabelli Utility Trust, The Gabelli Utilities Fund, The Gabelli Dividend Growth Fund, The Gabelli Focus Five Fund, The Comstock Capital Value Fund, The Gabelli Dividend and Income Trust, The Gabelli Global Utility &amp; Income
      Trust, The GAMCO Global Gold, Natural Resources, &amp; Income Trust, The GAMCO Natural Resources Gold &amp; Income Trust, The GDL Fund, Gabelli Enterprise Mergers &amp; Acquisitions Fund, The Gabelli ESG Fund, Inc., The Gabelli International Small
      Cap Fund, The Gabelli Healthcare &amp; Wellness <sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">Rx</sup> Trust, The Gabelli Global Small and Mid Cap Value Trust, Gabelli Value Plus+ Trust, Gabelli Merger Plus+ Trust Plc,&#160; The Gabelli Global Financial Services Fund, The Gabelli Global Mini
      Mites Fund, The Gabelli Go Anywhere Trust, The Gabelli Media Mogul Fund, The Gabelli Pet Parents&#8217; Fund, The Gabelli U.S. Treasury Money Market Fund, Bancroft Fund Ltd. and Ellsworth Growth &amp; Income Fund Ltd. (collectively, the &#8220;Funds&#8221;), which are
      registered investment companies.&#160; Gabelli Funds is also the investment adviser to The GAMCO International SICAV (sub-funds GAMCO Merger Arbitrage and GAMCO All Cap Value), a UCITS III vehicle.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">Teton Advisors, an investment adviser registered under the Advisers Act, provides discretionary advisory services to The TETON Westwood Mighty Mites<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">sm</sup> Fund, The TETON Westwood Income Fund,
      The TETON Westwood SmallCap Equity Fund, TETON Westwood Intermediate Bond Fund, and The TETON Westwood Mid-Cap Equity Fund.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">MJG Associates provides advisory services to private investment partnerships and offshore funds.&#160; Mario Gabelli is the sole shareholder, director and employee of MJG Associates.&#160;&#160; MJG Associates is the
      Investment Manager of Gabelli International Limited and Gabelli Fund, LDC.&#160; Mario J. Gabelli is the general partner of Gabelli Performance Partnership, LP.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">The Foundation is a private foundation.&#160; Mario Gabelli is the Chairman, a Trustee and the Investment Manager of the Foundation. Elisa M. Wilson is the President of the Foundation.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">LICT is a holding company with operating subsidiaries engaged primarily in the rural telephone industry. LICT actively pursues new business ventures and acquisitions. LICT makes investments in
      marketable securities to preserve capital and maintain liquidity for financing their business activities and acquisitions and are not engaged in the business of investing, or trading in securities. Mario J. Gabelli is the Chief Executive Officer, a
      director, and substantial shareholder of LICT.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">CIBL is a holding company with interests in telecommunications operations, primarily in the rural telephone industry. CIBL actively pursues new business ventures and acquisitions. CIBL makes investments
      in marketable securities to preserve capital and maintain liquidity for financing their business activities and acquisitions and are not engaged in the business of investing, or trading in securities. Mario J. Gabelli is a director, and substantial
      shareholder of CIBL.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">Mario Gabelli is the controlling stockholder, Chief Executive Officer and a director of GGCP and Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of GBL. He is the Executive Chairman of AC.&#160; Mario Gabelli is also a
      member of GGCP Holdings. Mario Gabelli is the controlling shareholder of Teton.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">The Reporting Persons do not admit that they constitute a group.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">GAMCO is a New York corporation and GBL, MGH and Teton Advisors are Delaware corporations, each having its principal business office at One Corporate Center, Rye, New York 10580. GGCP is a Wyoming
      corporation and AC and GCIA are Delaware corporations each having its principal business office 191 Mason Street, Greenwich, CT 06830.&#160;&#160; GGCP Holdings is a Delaware limited liability corporation having its principal business office at 191 Mason
      Street, Greenwich, CT 06830.&#160; G.research is a Delaware limited liability company having its principal officers at One Corporate Center, Rye, New York 10580.&#160; Gabelli Funds is a New York limited liability company having its principal business office
      at One Corporate Center, Rye, New York 10580.&#160; MJG Associates is a Connecticut corporation having its principal business office at 191 Mason Street, Greenwich, CT 06830.&#160; The Foundation is a Nevada corporation having its principal offices at 165 West
      Liberty Street, Reno, Nevada 89501.&#160; LICT is a Delaware corporation having its principal place of business as 401 Theodore Fremd Avenue, Rye, New York 10580. CIBL, Inc. is a Delaware corporation having its principal place of business as 165 West
      Liberty Street, Suite 220, Reno, NV 89501.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">For information required by instruction C to Schedule 13D with respect to the executive officers and directors of the foregoing entities and other related persons (collectively, &#8220;Covered Persons&#8221;),
      reference is made to Schedule I annexed hereto and incorporated herein by reference.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">(d) &#8211; Not applicable.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">(e) &#8211; Not applicable.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left;"><font style="display: inline-block; text-indent: 0px; font-size: 1px; width: 72pt" id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab">&#160;</font>(f) &#8211; Reference is made to Schedule I hereto.</div>

    <div style="text-align: left;">Item 4.<font style="display: inline-block; text-indent: 0px; font-size: 1px; width: 108pt" id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab">&#160;</font><u>Purpose of Transaction</u></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 72pt;">Item 4 to Schedule 13D is amended, in pertinent part, as follows:</div>
    <div style="text-align: left;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Today, GAMCO, on behalf of its investment advisory clients, sent notice to the Issuer of its intent to nominate Mr. Timothy E. Baxter as a candidate for election by shareholders to the Board
      of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of the Issuer at the Issuer's 2020 Annual Meeting of Shareholders (&#8220;Annual Meeting&#8221;).&#160; A copy of the notice is attached as Exhibit A.&#160; The intent to nominate Mr. Baxter is in addition to GAMCO&#8217;s previously announced intent
      to nominate Mr. Sugarman, Mr. Elliott, Mr. Abel, Mr. Putnam, Mr. Lisman and Mr. Liebau as candidates for election by shareholders to the Board of the Issuer at the Annual Meeting.</div>
    <div style="text-align: left;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;According to the Issuer, the deadline for shareholders to submit director nominations for consideration at the Annual Meeting is February 3, 2020.&#160; GAMCO&#8217;s Proxy Voting Committee (the &#8220;PVC&#8221;) is
      submitting today&#8217;s nomination notice in order to preserve GAMCO&#8217;s right to nominate candidates at the Annual Meeting, as the PVC continues to evaluate the situation.</div>

      Voting Committee of each Fund shall respectively vote that Fund&#8217;s shares, (iii) at any time, the Proxy Voting Committee of each such Fund may take and exercise in its sole discretion the entire voting power with respect to the shares held by such
